(src)="99929"> ↑ Occasionally , publishers erroneously assign an ISBN to more than one title—the first edition of The Ultimate Alphabet and The Ultimate Alphabet Workbook have the same ISBN , 0-8050-0076-3 .
(src)="99930"> Conversely , books are published with several ISBNs : A German second-language edition of Emil und die Detektive has the ISBNs 87-23-90157-8 ( Denmark ) , 0-8219-1069-8 ( United States ) , 91-21-15628-X ( Sweden ) , 0-85048-548-7 ( United Kingdom ) and 3-12-675495-3 ( Germany ) . ↑ In some cases , books sold only as sets share ISBNs .
(src)="99931"> For example , the Vance Integral Edition used only two ISBNs for 44 books .

(src)="99954"> Retrieved 29 April 2014 . ↑ Some books have several codes in the first block : e.g. A. M. Yaglom 's Correlation Theory ... , published by Springer Verlag , has two ISBNs , 0-387-96331-6 and 3-540-96331-6 .
(src)="99955"> Though Springer 's 387 and 540 codes are different for English ( 0 ) and German ( 3 ) ; the same item number 96331 produces the same check digit : 6 .
(src)="99956"> Springer uses 431 as their publisher code for Japanese ( 4 ) and 4-431-96331- ? would also have check digit ? = 6 .
(src)="99957"> Other Springer books in English have publisher code 817 , and 0-817-96331- ? would also get check digit ? = 6 .
(src)="99958"> This suggests special considerations were made for assigning Springer 's publisher codes , as random assignments of different publisher codes would not lead the same item number to get the same check digit every time .
(src)="99959"> Finding publisher codes for English and German , say , with this effect amounts to solving a linear equation in modular arithmetic . ↑ The international ISBN agency 's ISBN User 's Manual says : " The ten-digit number is divided into four parts of variable length , which must be separated clearly , by hyphens or spaces " although omission of separators is permitted for internal data processing .
(src)="99960"> If present , hyphens must be correctly placed ; see ISBN hyphenation definition .
(src)="99961"> The actual definition for hyphenation contains more than 220 different registration group elements with each one broken down into a few to several ranges for the length of the registrant element ( more than 1,000 total ) .
(src)="99962"> The document defining the ranges , listed by agency , is 29 pages . ↑ Canada , Library and Archives .

(src)="100018"> Miami Edison High School is a secondary school located at 6161 NW 5th Court in the Little Haiti neighborhood of Miami , Florida , USA .
(src)="100019"> It is part of the Miami-Dade County Public Schools system .
(src)="100020"> Its provost is Dr. Pablo G. Ortiz .
(trg)="92"> Lekòl Segondè Miami Edison  ( Miami Edison High School an angle )  se yon lekòl nan katye Ti Ayiti nan  Miyami pou elèv yo ki gen laj katòz a diznèf .
(trg)="93"> Li sitiye nan ri  5th Court ak lekòl la se yon pati de sistèm  Lekòl Leta Miami-Dade County .
(src)="100021"> Miami Edison , a low-income inner city school , As of 2011[update ] was known for historically having the largest Haitian American student population of any Miami-Dade public school.[1 ]
(trg)="94"> Lekòl la gen anpil anpil moun ayisyen .
(trg)="95"> Nan 2008 , 240 de 1150 elèv an total te itilize angle kòm dezyèm lang .
(src)="100022"> After the 2010 Haiti earthquake occurred , the MDCPS expected that there would be a large influx of students to Miami Edison .
(src)="100023"> Ultimately only six earthquake survivors enrolled there , with other students enrolling at other high schools.[1 ]

(src)="100040"> Nea Salamis Famagusta FC or Nea Salamina Famagusta FC ( Greek : Νέα Σαλαμίνα Αμμοχώστου ) is a professional football club based in Ammochostos ( also known by its romanized name , Famagusta ) , Cyprus .
(src)="100041"> It has been a refugee club since the 1974 Turkish invasion of Cyprus , when Turkey occupied the northern part of the island .
(src)="100042"> The club is temporarily based in Larnaca .

(src)="101125"> Yaa Asantewaa in batakarikese ( ceremonial war dress ) in an undated photograph .
(trg)="1189"> Yaa Asantewaa nan batakarikese ( rad gerye seromonyal ) nan yon foto san dat .
(src)="101126"> Yaa Asantewaa ( c.
(src)="101127"> 1840 – 17 October 1921 ) ( pronounced /ˈjɑː ɑːsɑːn.teɪ.wə/ ) was appointed queen mother of Ejisu in the Ashanti Empire—now part of modern-day Ghana—by her brother Nana Akwasi Afrane Okpese , the Ejisuhene—or ruler of Ejisu .
(src)="101128"> In 1900 , she led the Ashanti rebellion known as the War of the Golden Stool , also known as the Yaa Asantewaa war , against British colonialism.[1 ]
(trg)="1190"> Yaa Asantewaa ( c .
(trg)="1191"> 1840 – 17 oktòb 1921 ) ( pwononse / ˈjɑː ɑːsɑːn.teɪ.wə / ) te vin  renn  Ejisu nan Lanpi  Ashanti — ki fè pati de peyi  Gana  jodi-a — apre frèl Nana Akwasi Afrane Okpese , Ejisuhene — oswa chèf nan Ejisu te vin bal tit la .
(trg)="1192"> An 1900 , li te lidè rebelyon Ashanti yo rele Lagè Asantewaa oubyen Lagè Twòn Dore , kont kolon Angle . [ 1 ]
(src)="101129"> Born in 1840 in Besease in central Ghana , Yaa Asantewaa was the older of two children .
(src)="101130"> Her brother , Afrane Panin became the Chief of Edweso , a nearby community .
(src)="101131"> After a childhood without incident , she cultivated crops on the land around Boankra .
(src)="101132"> She entered a polygamous marriage with a man from Kumsai , with whom she had a daughter.[2 ]
(trg)="1193"> Yaa Asantewaa te fèt an 1840 nan Besease nan sant peyi Gana .
(trg)="1194"> Li te lene nan yon fanmi de timoun .  Frèl , Afrane Panin te vin Chèf nan Edweso , yon kominote ki tou pre .
(trg)="1195"> Apre yon anfans san problèm , li te kiltive latè ki sou nan alantou Boankra .
(trg)="1196"> Li te antre nan yon maryaj poligam ak yon nonm soti nan Kumsai e li te gen yon pitit fi avèl . [ 2 ]
(src)="101133"> During her brother 's reign , Yaa Asantewaa saw the Ashanti Confederacy go through a series of events that threatened its future , including civil war from 1883 to 1888 .
(src)="101134"> When her brother died in 1894 , Yaa Asantewaa used her right as Queen Mother to nominate her own grandson as Ejisuhene .
(src)="101135"> When the British exiled him in the Seychelles in 1896 , along with the King of Asante Prempeh I and other members of the Asante government , Yaa Asantewaa became regent of the Ejisu-Juaben District .
(src)="101136"> After the deportation of Prempeh I , the British governor-general of the Gold Coast , Frederick Hodgson , demanded the Golden Stool , the symbol of the Asante nation.[2 ] This request led to a secret meeting of the remaining members of the Asante government at Kumasi , to discuss how to secure the return of their king .
(src)="101137"> There was a disagreement among those present on how to go about this .
(src)="101138"> Yaa Asantewaa , who was present at this meeting , stood and addressed the members of the council with these now-famous words:[3 ]
(trg)="1197"> Pandan rèy frè li , Yaa Asantewaa te wè Konfederasyon Ashanti pase anpil tray ki menase lavni li , kankou yon gè sivil soti nan 1883 rive nan 1888 .
(trg)="1198"> Lè frèl te mouri an 1894 , Yaa Asantewaa itilize dwa li tankou Manman Renn peyi a pou nonmen pitit pitit li kòm Ejisuhene .
(trg)="1199"> Lè Angle yo depòtel nan la Sechèl  an 1896 , ansanm ak Wa Asante Prempeh I ak lòt manm nan gouvènman Asante an , Yaa Asantewaa te vin rejan nan distrik Ejisu-Juaben .
(trg)="1200"> Apre depòtasyon Prempeh I , gouvènè-jeneral Kòt Dò a , Frederick Hodgson  ki te yon blan Angle , te egzije oou yo remèt li twòn dore-a ki se senbòl nanchon Asante-a . [ 2 ]  Dikta sa-a te a te fè rès manm gouvènman Asante a reyini nan Kumasi pou diskite kijan pou yo fè wa yo tounen lakay li .
(trg)="1201"> Yo pat rive dakò sou kijan pou sa te fèt .
(trg)="1202"> Yaa Asantewaa , ki te prezan nan reyinyon sa a te kanpe poul pale ak manm konsèy la .
(trg)="1203"> Pawòl li nan okazyon sa-a vin selèb : [ 3 ]
(src)="101139"> " Now I have seen that some of you fear to go forward to fight for our king .
(src)="101140"> If it were the brave days of Osei Tutu , Okomfo Anokye and Opuki Ware , chiefs would not sit down to see their king taken without firing a shot .
(src)="101141"> No white man could have dared to speak to the Chief of Asante in the way the governor spoke to you chiefs this morning .
(src)="101142"> Is it true that the bravery of Asante is no more ?
(src)="101143"> I cannot believe it .
(src)="101144"> It cannot be !
(src)="101145"> I must say this : if you , the men of Asante , will not go forward , then we will .
(src)="101146"> I shall call upon my fellow women .
(src)="101147"> We will fight the white men .
(src)="101148"> We will fight till the last of us falls on the battlefield."[4 ]
(trg)="1204"> " Sanble gen nan nou ki pè batay pou wa nou .
(trg)="1205"> Mwen sonje epòk Osei Tutu , Okomfo Anokye ak Opuki Ware , epòk chèf ki pat kite moun vin atake wa nou .
(trg)="1206"> Pat gen okenn blan ki tap vin pèmèt li pale ak ak Chèf Asante jan gouvènè angle a te vin pal avèk nou maten an .
(trg)="1207"> Eske se ta vre Asante pa gen grenn ankò ?
(trg)="1208"> Mwen pa ka kwè sa .
(trg)="1209"> Li pa ka !
(trg)="1210"> Map sèmante : si gason vanyan Asante yo pap batay , en ben noumenm fanm nap degaje nou .
(trg)="1211"> Map rele fanm parèy mwen .
(trg)="1212"> Nou pral goumen kont nonm blan yo .  Nou pral goumen jouk nou tout tonbe sou chan batay la . " [ 4 ]
(src)="101149"> The next morning , 28 March 1900 , Yaa Asantewaa gathered her women together , followed by her shame-faced men .
(src)="101150"> With an army of some five thousand , she led the Asante Uprising , known as the War of the Golden Stool .
(src)="101151"> Supported by some of the other Asante nobility , she fought valiantly against the British.[4][5 ]
(trg)="1213"> Nan denmen maten , 28 Mas 1900 , Yaa Asantewaa rasanble fanm yo ansanm , ak tout gason ki deside swiv yo .
(trg)="1214"> Ak yon lame senk mil moun , li te dirije Soulèvman  Asante ke yon vin rele Lagè Twòn Dore a .
(trg)="1215"> Ak sipò  rès noblès Asante-a , li te goumen ak vanyans kont Britanik yo . [ 4 ] [ 5 ]
(src)="101152"> The confrontation of a woman , serving as political and military head of an empire , was foreign to British colonial troops in 19th-century Africa .
(src)="101153"> Yaa Asantewaa 's call upon the women of the Asante Empire is based on the political obligations of Akan women and their respective roles in legislative and judicial processes .
(src)="101154"> The hierarchy of male stools among the Akan people were complemented by female counterparts .
(src)="101155"> Within the village , elders known as ( mpanyimfo ) heads of the matrilineages , constituted with the village council known as the ôdekuro .
(src)="101156"> These women known as the mpanyinfo referred to aberewa or ôbaa panyin , to look after women 's affairs .
(src)="101157"> For every ôdekuro , an ôbaa panyin acted as the responsible party for the affairs of the women of the village and served as a member of the village council.[10 ]
(trg)="1216"> Konfwontasyon yon fanm ki tap sèvi kòm chèf politik ak militè yon anpi pat yon bagay lame kolon Angle te abitye nan 19yèm syèk .
(trg)="1217"> Jan Yaa Asantewaa te rasanble fanm nan peyi Akan an soti nan obligasyon politik fanm nan peyi Akan yo ki te gen wòl yo nan lajistis ak nan paleman .
(trg)="1218"> Yerachi twòn gason nan pèp Akan te ale men nan men ak fanm ki nan menm pozisyon .
(trg)="1219"> Nan lakou yo , granmoun fanm ki te rele mpanyimfo yo te travay tèt kole ak konsèy lakou a ki te rele  ôdekuro .
(trg)="1220"> Fanm mpanyinfo yo te travay ak  aberewa oswa ôbaa panyin , pou rezoud pwoblèm fanm .
(trg)="1221"> Pou chak ôdekuro , yon ôbaa panyin  te responsab zafè fanm yo nan vilaj la e te sèvi kòm yon manm nan konsèy vilaj la . [ 10 ]
(src)="101162"> The room believed to be Yaa Asantewaa 's Cell
(trg)="1222"> The room believed to be Yaa Asantewaa ' s Cell
(src)="101163"> Beginning in March 1900 , the rebellion laid siege to the fort at Kumasi where the British had sought refuge .
(src)="101164"> The fort still stands today as the Kumasi Fort and Military Museum .
(src)="101165"> After several months , the Gold Coast governor eventually sent a force of 1,400 to quell the rebellion .
(src)="101166"> During the course of this , Queen Yaa Asantewaa and 15 of her closest advisers were captured , and they too were sent into exile to the Seychelles.[6 ] The rebellion represented the final war in the Anglo-Asante series of wars that lasted throughout the 19th century .
(src)="101167"> On 1 January 1902 , the British were finally able to accomplish what the Asante army had denied them for almost a century , and the Asante empire was made a protectorate of the British crown.[7 ]
(trg)="1223"> An Mas 1900 , rebelyon an fè syèj Fò Kumasi a kote Angle yo te refijye .
(trg)="1224"> Fò a egziste toujou jodi-ae li rele Mize Militè Fò Kumasi .
(trg)="1225"> Apre plizyè mwa , Gouvènè Kot Dò a te voye yon fòs 1.400 moun pou kraze rebelyon an .
(trg)="1226"> Pandan tan sa-a , yo kaptire Larenn Yaa Asantewaa ak 15 nan konseye pwòch li , e yo te voye yo ann egzil nan lè Sechèl . [ 6 ]  Rebelyon an te reprezante batay final la nan yon seri de batay Anglo-Asante ki dire pandan 19e syèk .
(trg)="1227"> Nan premye janvye 1902 , Angle yo te fin pa akonpli sa lame Asanti te anpeche yo fè pandan yon syèk e lanpi Asanti te vin on protektora britanik . [ 7 ]
(src)="101168"> Yaa Asantewaa died in exile in the Seychelles on 17 October 1921 .
(src)="101169"> Three years after her death , on 27 December 1924 , Prempeh I and the other remaining members of the exiled Asante court were allowed to return to Asante .
(src)="101170"> Prempeh I made sure that the remains of Yaa Asantewaa and the other exiled Asantes were returned for a proper royal burial.[8 ] Yaa Asantewaa 's dream for an Asante free of British rule was realized on 6 March 1957 , when the Asante protectorate gained independence as part of Ghana , the first African nation in Subsaharan Africa to achieve this feat.[9 ]
(trg)="1228"> Yaa Asantewaa te mouri ann ekzil nan peyi Sechèl le 17 oktòb 1921 .
(trg)="1229"> Twa lane apre lanmò li , nan 27 desanm 1924 , Prempeh I ak lòt egzile noblès Asanti yo te retounen nan peyi yo .
(trg)="1230"> Prempeh I te fè kò Asantewaa ak lòt depòte Asante yo tounen nan peyi yo pou yon antèman wayal kòm sa dwa . [ 8 ]  Rèv Yaa Asantewaa pou yon peyi Asante san dominasyon kolon Angle te reyalize nan 6 Mas 1957 , lè pwotektora Asante a te pran endepandans ansanm ak rès peyi Gana , premye nasyon Afriken nan Lafrik Ginen ki akonpli sila . [ 9 ]

(src)="101374"> Violence against women ( VAW ) , also known as gender-based violence,[1 ] is , collectively , violent acts that are primarily or exclusively committed against women .
(src)="101375"> Sometimes considered a hate crime,[2][3][4 ] this type of violence targets a specific group with the victim 's gender as a primary motive .
(src)="101376"> This type of violence is gender-based , meaning that the acts of violence are committed against women expressly because they are women .
(src)="101377"> The UN Declaration on the Elimination of Violence Against Women states that :
(trg)="1411"> Vyolans kont fanm ( VAW ) , tou li te ye kòm vyolans ki baze sou sèks , [ 1 ] se , kolektivman , zak vyolan ki se sitou oswa sèlman komèt kont fanm yo .
(trg)="1412"> Sa a ki kalite vyolans sib yon gwoup espesifik ak viktim nan sèks kòm yon motif nan prensipal .
(trg)="1413"> Sa a ki kalite vyolans ki baze sou sèks , ki vle di ke zak vyolans yo ap komèt kont fanm yo ekspreseman paske yo se fanm .
(trg)="1414"> NASYONZINI nan Deklarasyon sou Eliminasyon Vyolans Kont Fanm eta yo ki : [ 3 ]
(src)="101378"> Violence against women can fit into several broad categories .
(src)="101379"> These include violence carried out by " individuals " as well as " states " .
(src)="101380"> Some of the forms of violence perpetrated by individuals are rape ; domestic violence ; sexual harassment ; coercive use of contraceptives ; female infanticide ; prenatal sex selection ; obstetric violence and mob violence ; as well as harmful customary or traditional practices such as honor killings , dowry violence , female genital mutilation , marriage by abduction and forced marriage .
(src)="101381"> Some forms of violence are perpetrated or condoned by the state such as war rape ; sexual violence and sexual slavery during conflict ; forced sterilization ; forced abortion ; violence by the police and authoritative personnel ; stoning and flogging .
(src)="101382"> Many forms of VAW , such as trafficking in women and forced prostitution are often perpetrated by organized criminal networks.[7 ]
(trg)="1415"> Gen kèk nan fòm yo nan vyolans komèt pa moun ki yo se kadejak ; vyolans domestik ; arasman seksyèl ; koèrsitif itilize nan kontraseptif ; fi enfantisid ; prenatal sèks seleksyon ; obstetrik vyolans ak vyolans foul ; kòm byen ke danjere òdinè oswa pratik tradisyonèl tankou asasinay onè , dot vyolans , fanm jenital mutilasyon , maryaj pa fè anlèvman ak fòse maryaj .
(trg)="1416"> Kèk fòm vyolans yo komèt oswa tolere pa eta a tankou lagè kadejak ; vyolans seksyèl ak esklavaj seksyèl pandan konfli ; fòse esterilizasyon ; fòse avòtman ; vyolans nan lapolis la ak autorité pèsonèl ; kout ak fustigasyon .
(trg)="1417"> Anpil fòm nan VAW , tankou trafik fanm ak pwostitisyon fòse yo souvan pèpetre ensidan ki te òganize kriminèl rezo . [ 7 ]

(src)="101657"> " Gender-neutrality and gender equality : comparing and contrasting policy responses to ' domestic violence ' in Finland and Scotland " .
(src)="101658"> Scottish Affairs .
(src)="101659"> Edinburgh University Press .
(src)="101660"> 48 ( 1 ) : 85–107 . doi:10.3366/scot.2004.0043 .
(src)="101661"> Pdf . ↑ Danish , Swedish , Finnish and Norwegian sections of Amnesty International ( March 2010 ) , " Rape and human rights in Finland " , in Danish , Swedish , Finnish and Norwegian sections of Amnesty International , Case closed : rape and human rights in the Nordic countries , Amnesty International , pp.  89–91 , Finland is repeatedly reminded of its widespread problem of violence against women and recommended to take more efficient measures to deal with the situation .
(src)="101662"> International criticism concentrates on the lack of measures to combat violence against women in general and in particular on the lack of a national action plan to combat such violence and on the lack of legislation on domestic violence . ( ... )
(src)="101663"> Compared to Sweden , Finland has been slower to reform legislation on violence against women .
(src)="101664"> In Sweden , domestic violence was already illegal in 1864 , while in Finland such violence was not outlawed until 1970 , over a hundred years later .
(src)="101665"> In Sweden the punishment of victims of incest was abolished in 1937 , but not until 1971 in Finland .
(src)="101666"> Rape within marriage was criminalised in Sweden in 1962 , but the equivalent Finnish legislation only came into force in 1994 – making Finland one of the last European countries to criminalise marital rape .
(src)="101667"> In addition , assaults taking place on private property did not become impeachable offences in Finland until 1995 .
(src)="101668"> Only in 1997 did victims of sexual offences and domestic violence in Finland become entitled to government-funded counselling and support services for the duration of their court cases .  CS1 maint : Multiple names : authors list ( link ) Pdf . ↑ Bott , Sarah ; Guedes , Alessandra ; Goodwin , Mary ; Mendoza , Jennifer Adams ( 2012 ) .

(trg)="1675"> " Gender-neutrality and gender equality : comparing and contrasting policy responses to ' domestic violence ' in Finland and Scotland " .
(trg)="1676"> Scottish Affairs .
(trg)="1677"> Edinburgh University Press .
(trg)="1678"> 48 ( 1 ) : 85 – 107. doi : 10.3366 / scot.2004.0043.
(trg)="1679"> Pdf . ↑ Danish , Swedish , Finnish and Norwegian sections of Amnesty International ( March 2010 ) , " Rape and human rights in Finland " , in Danish , Swedish , Finnish and Norwegian sections of Amnesty International , Case closed : rape and human rights in the Nordic countries , Amnesty International , pp.  89 – 91 , Finland is repeatedly reminded of its widespread problem of violence against women and recommended to take more efficient measures to deal with the situation .
(trg)="1680"> International criticism concentrates on the lack of measures to combat violence against women in general and in particular on the lack of a national action plan to combat such violence and on the lack of legislation on domestic violence . ( ... )
(trg)="1681"> Compared to Sweden , Finland has been slower to reform legislation on violence against women .
(trg)="1682"> In Sweden , domestic violence was already illegal in 1864 , while in Finland such violence was not outlawed until 1970 , over a hundred years later .
(trg)="1683"> In Sweden the punishment of victims of incest was abolished in 1937 , but not until 1971 in Finland .
(trg)="1684"> Rape within marriage was criminalised in Sweden in 1962 , but the equivalent Finnish legislation only came into force in 1994 – making Finland one of the last European countries to criminalise marital rape .
(trg)="1685"> In addition , assaults taking place on private property did not become impeachable offences in Finland until 1995 .
(trg)="1686"> Only in 1997 did victims of sexual offences and domestic violence in Finland become entitled to government-funded counselling and support services for the duration of their court cases .  CS1 maint : Multiple names : authors list ( link ) Pdf . ↑ Bott , Sarah ; Guedes , Alessandra ; Goodwin , Mary ; Mendoza , Jennifer Adams ( 2012 ) .

(trg)="2457"> 1 2 " Side Effects of Penicillin for Dogs " .
(src)="102457"> Diarrhea , also spelled diarrhoea , is the condition of having at least three loose or liquid bowel movements each day .
(src)="102458"> It often lasts for a few days and can result in dehydration due to fluid loss .
(src)="102459"> Signs of dehydration often begin with loss of the normal stretchiness of the skin and irritable behaviour .
(src)="102460"> This can progress to decreased urination , loss of skin color , a fast heart rate , and a decrease in responsiveness as it becomes more severe .
(src)="102461"> Loose but non-watery stools in babies who are breastfed , however , may be normal.[2 ]
(trg)="2458"> Dyare se kondisyon an nan li te gen omwen twa ki lage oswa likid mouvman nan entesten chak jou .
(trg)="2459"> Li souvan dire pou yon kèk jou epi yo ka rezilta nan dezidratasyon akòz pèdi likid .
(trg)="2460"> Siy dezidratasyon souvan kòmanse ak pèt nan nòmal stretchiness nan po a ak chimerik konpòtman .
(trg)="2461"> Sa a ka pwogrè pou diminye pipi , pèt nan koulè po , yon vit vitès batman kè , ak yon diminisyon nan reyaksyon yo kòm li vin pi grav .
(trg)="2462"> Ki lach men , ki pa peye-dlo sèl nan ti bebe ki tete manman , sepandan , pouvwa dwe nòmal . [ 2 ]
(src)="102462"> About 1.7 to 5  billion cases of diarrhea occur per year.[2][5][9 ] It is most common in developing countries , where young children get diarrhea on average three times a year.[2 ] Total deaths from diarrhea are estimated at 1.26  million in 2013 – down from 2.58  million in 1990.[10 ] In 2012 , it was the second most common cause of deaths in children younger than five ( 0.76 million or 11%).[2][11 ] Frequent episodes of diarrhea are also a common cause of malnutrition and the most common cause in those younger than five years of age.[2 ] Other long term problems that can result include stunted growth and poor intellectual development.[11 ]
(trg)="2463"> Jenn timoun yo jwenn dyare sou mwayèn twa fwa yon ane . [ 2 ] Total moun ki mouri soti nan dyare yo estime nan 1.26 milyon dola nan 2013 – desann soti nan 2.58 milyon dola nan ane 1990 . [ 10 ] Nan 2012 , li te dezyèm kòz ki pi komen nan lanmò nan timoun ki pi piti pase senk ( 0.76 milyon dola oswa 11 % ) . [ 2 ] [ 11 ] Souvan epizòd dyare yo tou se yon koz komen nan malnitrisyon ak kòz ki pi komen nan moun ki gen mwens pase senk ane nan laj . [ 2 ] Lòt tèm long nan pwoblèm ki ka lakòz gen ladan rachòt kwasans ak pòv devlopman entelektyèl . [ 11 ]
(src)="102463"> Diarrheal disease may have a negative impact on both physical fitness and mental development .
(src)="102464"> " Early childhood malnutrition resulting from any cause reduces physical fitness and work productivity in adults,"[16 ] and diarrhea is a primary cause of childhood malnutrition.[17 ] Further , evidence suggests that diarrheal disease has significant impacts on mental development and health ; it has been shown that , even when controlling for helminth infection and early breastfeeding , children who had experienced severe diarrhea had significantly lower scores on a series of tests of intelligence.[16][18 ]
(trg)="2464"> Dyare se yon kòz prensipal nan malnitrisyon timoun . [ 17 ] pli Lwen , prèv sijere ke dyare , maladi a te gen enpak siyifikatif sou devlopman mantal ak sante ; li te montre ke , menm lè yo kontwole pou helminth enfeksyon ak byen bonè bay tete , timoun yo ki te fè eksperyans grav dyare ki te siyifikativman pi ba nòt sou yon seri de tès yo nan entèlijans . [ 16 ] [ 18 ]
(src)="102465"> While antibiotics are beneficial in certain types of acute diarrhea , they are usually not used except in specific situations.[76][77 ] There are concerns that antibiotics may increase the risk of hemolytic uremic syndrome in people infected with Escherichia coli O157:H7.[78 ] In resource-poor countries , treatment with antibiotics may be beneficial.[77 ] However , some bacteria are developing antibiotic resistance , particularly Shigella.[79 ] Antibiotics can also cause diarrhea , and antibiotic-associated diarrhea is the most common adverse effect of treatment with general antibiotics .
(trg)="2465"> Antibyotik yo se benefisye nan sèten kalite dyare egi yo . [ 76 ] [ 77 ] Sepandan , gen kèk bakteri ap devlope antibyotik rezistans , patikilyèman Shigella . [ 79 ] Antibyotik yo kapab lakòz tou dyare , ak antibyotik-ki asosye dyare , se yo ki pi komen efè negatif nan tretman ak jeneral antibyotik .

(src)="102997"> Diseases
(trg)="2965"> konsiltasyon maladi
(src)="102998"> Therapies
(trg)="2966"> Tretman
(src)="102999"> Gynaecology or gynecology ( see spelling differences ) is the medical practice dealing with the health of the female reproductive systems ( vagina , uterus , and ovaries ) and the breasts .
(src)="103000"> Literally , outside medicine , the term means " the science of women " .
(src)="103001"> Its counterpart is andrology , which deals with medical issues specific to the male reproductive system .
(trg)="2967"> Jinekoloji  se pratik medikal ki gen rapò ak sante nan nan sistèm repwodiksyon fanm nan ( vajen , matris , ak ovè ) ak tete . 
(src)="103002"> In some countries , women must first see a general practitioner ( GP ; also known as a family practitioner (FP)) prior to seeing a gynaecologist .
(src)="103003"> If their condition requires training , knowledge , surgical procedure , or equipment unavailable to the GP , the patient is then referred to a gynaecologist .
(src)="103004"> In the United States , however , law and many health insurance plans allow gynaecologists to provide primary care in addition to aspects of their own specialty .
(src)="103005"> With this option available , some women opt to see a gynaecological surgeon for non-gynaecological problems without another physician 's referral .
(trg)="2968"> Nan Peyi Etazini  lalwa , ak anpil asirans sante plan pèmèt gynaecologists bay swen primè yo anplis de sa yo aspè nan pwòp espesyalite .
(trg)="2969"> Ak opsyon sa a disponib , gen kèk fanm refize nou bay enfòmasyon pou wè yon gynaecological chirijyen pou ki pa peye-gynaecological pwoblèm san yon lòt doktè a referans .
(src)="103006"> As in all of medicine , the main tools of diagnosis are clinical history and examination .
(src)="103007"> Gynaecological examination is quite intimate , more so than a routine physical exam .
(src)="103008"> It also requires unique instrumentation such as the speculum .
(src)="103009"> The speculum consists of two hinged blades of concave metal or plastic which are used to retract the tissues of the vagina and permit examination of the cervix , the lower part of the uterus located within the upper portion of the vagina .
(src)="103010"> Gynaecologists typically do a bimanual examination ( one hand on the abdomen and one or two fingers in the vagina ) to palpate the cervix , uterus , ovaries and bony pelvis .
(src)="103011"> It is not uncommon to do a rectovaginal examination for complete evaluation of the pelvis , particularly if any suspicious masses are appreciated .
(src)="103012"> Male gynaecologists may have a female chaperone for their examination .
(src)="103013"> An abdominal or vaginal ultrasound can be used to confirm any abnormalities appreciated with the bimanual examination or when indicated by the patient 's history .
(trg)="2970"> Prensipal la zouti yo nan dyagnostik yo nan klinik , istwa a ak egzamen an .
(trg)="2971"> Gynaecological egzamen se byen alèz , plis konsa pase yon egzamen fizik woutin .
(trg)="2972"> Li egzije tou pou inik instrumentation tankou vè .
(trg)="2973"> An vè konsiste de de vrata za lam nan konkav metal oswa plastik ki yo te itilize yo retire tisi yo nan vajen an ak pèmi egzamen an nan kòl matrisla , pati ki pi ba nan matris la ki sitiye nan pati anwo nan vajen an .
(trg)="2974"> Gynaecologists tipikman fè yon bimanual egzamen ( yon men sou vant la ak youn oswa de dwèt nan vajen ) yo palpate kòl matris la , matris la , ovè yo ak zo basen .
(trg)="2975"> Gason gynaecologists ka gen yon fi chapron pou egzamen yo . 
(src)="103014"> Surgery , however , is the mainstay of gynaecological therapy .
(src)="103015"> For historical and political reasons , gynaecologists were previously not considered " surgeons " , although this point has always been the source of some controversy .
(src)="103016"> Modern advancements in both general surgery and gynaecology , however , have blurred many of the once rigid lines of distinction .
(src)="103017"> The rise of sub-specialties within gynaecology which are primarily surgical in nature ( for example urogynaecology and gynaecological oncology ) have strengthened the reputations of gynaecologists as surgical practitioners , and many surgeons and surgical societies have come to view gynaecologists as comrades of sorts .
(src)="103018"> As proof of this changing attitude , gynaecologists are now eligible for fellowship in both the American College of Surgeons and Royal Colleges of Surgeons , and many newer surgical textbooks include chapters on ( at least basic ) gynaecological surgery .
(trg)="2976"> Operasyon se pafwa nesesè .
(src)="103019"> Almost all modern gynaecologists are also obstetricians ( see obstetrics and gynaecology ) .
(src)="103020"> In many areas , the specialities of gynaecology and obstetrics overlap .
(trg)="2977"> Nan anpil zòn , espesyalite a nan jinekoloji ak obstetrik sipèpoze .
(src)="103021"> As with all surgical specialties , gynaecologists may employ medical or surgical therapies ( or many times , both ) , depending on the exact nature of the problem that they are treating .
(src)="103022"> Pre- and post-operative medical management will often employ many standard drug therapies , such as antibiotics , diuretics , antihypertensives , and antiemetics .
(src)="103023"> Additionally , gynaecologists make frequent use of specialized hormone-modulating therapies ( such as Clomifene citrate and hormonal contraception ) to treat disorders of the female genital tract that are responsive to pituitary or gonadal signals .
(trg)="2978"> Tretman ka antibyotik , medikaman pèdi dlo , antiipèrtanseur , ak medikaman yo anpeche vomisman .
(trg)="2979"> Pafwa òmòn yo te itilize .
(src)="103024"> Infections in infants in resource-limited settings
(trg)="2980"> Depans
(src)="103025"> Amoxicillin , also spelled amoxycillin , is an antibiotic useful for the treatment of a number of bacterial infections.[2 ] It is the first line treatment for middle ear infections .
(src)="103026"> It may also be used for strep throat , pneumonia , skin infections , and urinary tract infections among others.[2 ] It is taken by mouth , or less commonly by injection.[2][3 ]
(trg)="2981"> Amoxicillin , tou eple amoxycillin , se yon antibyotik ki itil pou tretman bakteri ak enfeksyon . [ 2 ] Li se te pran nan bouch , oubyen mwens souvan pa piki . [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
(src)="103027"> Common side effects include nausea and rash.[2 ] It may also increase the risk of yeast infections and , when used in combination with clavulanic acid , diarrhea.[4 ] It should not be used in those who are allergic to penicillin .
(src)="103028"> While usable in those with kidney problems , the dose may need to be decreased .
(src)="103029"> Its use in pregnancy and breastfeeding does not appear to be harmful.[2 ]
(trg)="2982"> Efè segondè komen enkli noze ak gratèl . [ 2 ] Li pouvwa tou ogmante risk la nan enfeksyon ledven epi , lè yo itilize nan konbinezon ak  dyare . [ 4 ] Li pa ta dwe itilize nan tout moun ki fè alèji ak penisilin .
(trg)="2983"> Sèvi ak li yo nan gwosès ak bay tete pa parèt yo dwe danjere . [ 2 ]

(trg)="3074"> PMID  20687896. doi : 10.1042 / BSR20100027 . 
(src)="103118"> The risk of ovarian cancer increases in women who have ovulated more over their lifetime .
(src)="103119"> This includes those who have never had children , those who begin ovulation at a younger age or reach menopause at an older age.[3 ] Other risk factors include hormone therapy after menopause , fertility medication , and obesity.[4][5 ] Factors that decrease risk include hormonal birth control , tubal ligation , and breast feeding.[5 ] About 10 % of cases are related to inherited genetic risk ; women with mutations in the genes BRCA1 or BRCA2 have about a 50 % chance of developing the disease.[3 ] The most common type of ovarian cancer , comprising more than 95 % of cases , is ovarian carcinoma.[3 ] There are five main subtypes of ovarian carcinoma , of which high-grade serous carcinoma is the most common.[3 ] These tumors are believed to start in the cells covering the ovaries,[3 ] though some may form at the Fallopian tubes.[13 ] Less common types of ovarian cancer include germ cell tumors and sex cord stromal tumors.[3 ] A diagnosis of ovarian cancer is confirmed through a biopsy of tissue , usually removed during surgery.[1 ]
(trg)="3075"> Faktè ki diminye risk gen ladan ormon pou kontwòl nesans , toubal litij , ak bay tete . [ 5 ] Apeprè 10 % nan ka yo ki gen rapò ak jenetik eritye risk ; fanm ak mitasyon nan jèn yo BRCA1 oswa BRCA2 gen sou yon 50 % chans pou yo devlope maladi-a . [ 3 ] kalite ki pi komen pou kansè nan ovè , comprenant plis pase 95 % nan ka yo , se nan ovè malfijyen . (src)="103120"> Early signs and symptoms of ovarian cancer may be absent or subtle .
(src)="103121"> In most cases , symptoms exist for several months before being recognized and diagnosed.[16][17 ] Symptoms can be misdiagnosed as irritable bowel syndrome.[18 ] The early stages of ovarian cancer tend to be painless .
(src)="103122"> Symptoms can vary based on the subtype.[16 ] Low malignant potential ( LMP ) tumors , also known as borderline tumors , do not cause an increase in CA125 levels and are not identifiable with an ultrasound .
(src)="103123"> The typical symptoms of an LMP tumor can include abdominal distension or pelvic pain .
(src)="103124"> Particularly large masses tend to be benign or borderline.[19][16 ]
(trg)="3076"> Byen bonè siy ak sentòm yo nan kansè nan ovè yo pouvwa dwe absan oswa sibtil .
(trg)="3077"> Nan pifò ka , jan ou santi ou egziste pou plizyè mwa anvan ke yo te rekonèt ak dyagnostike . [ 16 ] [ 17 ] Sentòm yo ka misdiagnosed tankou sendwòm entesten chimerik . [ 18 ] premye etap Yo byen bonè nan kansè nan ovè yo gen tandans yo dwe fèt san doulè .
(trg)="3078"> Sentòm yo ka varye ki baze sou subtip . [ 16 ] 
(src)="103125"> Hormonal conditions such as polycystic ovary syndrome and endometriosis are associated with ovarian cancer , but the link is not completely confirmed.[18 ] Postmenopausal hormone replacement therapy ( HRT ) with estrogen likely increases the risk of ovarian cancer .
(src)="103126"> The association has not been confirmed in a large-scale study,[19][26 ] but notable studies including the Million Women Study have supported this link .
(src)="103127"> Postmenopausal HRT with combined estrogen and progesterone may increase contemporaneous risk if used for over 5 years , but this risk returns to normal after cessation of therapy.[24 ] Estrogen HRT with or without progestins increases the risk of endometrioid and serous tumors but lowers the risk of mucinous tumors .
(src)="103128"> Higher doses of estrogen increase this risk.[21 ] Endometriosis is another risk factor for ovarian cancer,[24 ] as is pain with menstruation .
(src)="103129"> Endometriosis is associated with clear-cell and endometrioid subtypes , low-grade serous tumors , stage I and II tumors , grade 1 tumors , and lower mortality.[21 ]
(trg)="3079"> Ormon kondisyon tankou polisistik sendwòm ovè ak andometryoz se ki asosye avèk kansè nan ovè , men lyen ki se pa konplètman konfime . [ 18 ]

(trg)="3408"> Check date values in : | access-date = ( help )
(src)="103466"> The growing mass may cause pain if ovarian torsion develops .
(src)="103467"> Symptoms can be caused by a mass pressing on the other abdominopelvic organs or from metastases.[16][20][21 ] If these symptoms start to occur more often or more severely than usual , especially after no significant history of such symptoms , ovarian cancer is considered.[16][19 ] Metastases may cause a Sister Mary Joseph nodule.[21 ] Rarely , teratomas can cause growing teratoma syndrome or peritoneal gliomatosis.[21 ] Some experience menometrorrhagia and abnormal vaginal bleeding after menopause in most cases .
(src)="103468"> Other common symptoms include hirsutism , abdominal pain , virilization , and an adnexal mass.[22 ]
(trg)="3409"> An mas k ap grandi yo ka lakòz doulè , si ovè torsion devlope .
(trg)="3410"> Sentòm yo ka ki te koze pa yon mas peze sou lòt abdominopelvic ògàn oswa nan metastaz . [ 16 ] [ 20 ] [ 21 ] Si sentòm sa yo kòmanse rive pi souvan oswa plis grav pase nòmal , espesyalman apre pa gen okenn istwa enpòtan nan sentòm sa yo , kansè nan ovè a se konsidere kòm . [ 16 ] [ 19 ] Kèk fanm eksperyans menometrorrhagia ak pa nòmal nan vajen senyen apre menopoz nan pifò ka yo .
(trg)="3411"> Lòt sentòm komen yo gen ladan irsutism , doulè nan vant , virilization , ak yon adnexal mas . [ 22 ]

(src)="103675"> Toussaint was chief surgeon at Howard University for the liver transplant center .
(src)="103676"> Prior to this , she trained under Thomas Starzl at the University of Pittsburgh Medical School for three years .
(src)="103677"> In 1997 , she left Howard University Hospital .
(src)="103678"> She wrote an autobiography , Never Question the Miracle : A Surgeon ’s Story , in which she describes the prediction of a Vodun priest who predicted she would be a doctor when she grew up .
(src)="103679"> As founder of the National Transplant Foundation Inc. she works with those that need assistance to defray the cost of organ transplants .

(src)="103682"> Cracked nipples that happens when a mother breastfeeds her infant .
(src)="103683"> This can happen for many reasons .
(src)="103684"> When a mother gets cracked nipples it can be very painful .
(src)="103685"> The nipples can be in sore , dry , chapped or bleeding .
(src)="103686"> When the baby is breastfeeding the cracked nipple can cause great pain .
(src)="103687"> Many times this severe pain will make the mother stop breastfeeding.The crack looks like a cut across the tip of the nipple.[1 ] Cracked nipples can sometimes be treated.[2 ]
(trg)="3566"> Fann pwent tete ki rive lè tete tibebe l .
